I have adrenal insufficiency which is the life threatening  illness  that causes me to have hypoglycemic episodes repeatedly.  I have gone into shock, seizures and yes low glucose related Comas. Adrenal insufficiency is different than diabetes and how it affects blood sugar, but being that especially here in America type 2 diabetes is a huge problem and there are a lot of individuals who struggle with type 1 diabetes requiring permanent insulin pumps our community really struggles.  I take absolutely no offense to the theme of this product line nor any of the names of the colors but I have to be honest every time I hear coma I cringe a little bit.  I would just love to see some donations to a cause that would help this community. You have such a wide platform and you could take something as beautiful as this collection and turn it into something just as beautiful by helping people diagnosed with type 1 diabetes, Type 2 diabetes or adrenal insufficiency like myself.
